New Motorbike Record

Created by a German, Schuni

Reuters, Berlin, 20th: Today, German Schuni rode a two-wheeled motorbike and traveled one mile in 26.38 seconds, averaging 219.618 kilometers per hour. This is the absolute world record. The previous record set by Englishman Wright was 218.18 miles per hour.

Rumors of Briand's Assassination

Townspeople Are Like Grass and Trees, Startled at the Slightest Sound

Ending in a False Alarm

National News Agency, Paris, 20th: A small town in France, only a hundred miles from Paris, suddenly spread the rumor that Foreign Minister Briand was assassinated by an Italian thug in Geneva. Troops from a neighboring town even marched through the town, and the people were in a panic. It was falsely rumored that the government had ordered mobilization, and the local authorities rashly ordered the church to ring the bell to gather the masses. As a result, the whole town was in turmoil, and women and children cried, trying to prevent the conscription of young men within their reserve military service period. It was not until several hours later that a telephone call from Paris to the town revealed that it was purely a false alarm, and the disturbance subsided. Although this incident is foolish and ridiculous, it is enough to show the restlessness of the people's hearts in France and throughout Europe at the moment.

Important Domestic News

The Central Government Holds a

Commemoration for the Tenth Anniversary of Zhu Zhixin's Martyrdom

At 9:00 AM on the 21st, the Central Party Headquarters held a commemoration for the tenth anniversary of Zhu Zhixin's martyrdom in the auditorium. Central Committee members Hu Hanmin, Gu Yingfen, Wang Zhengting, Chen Bulei, Li Wenfan, Ke Xing'e, and Miao Peicheng, among others, and representatives from various agencies, totaling about three or four hundred people, attended. Hu Hanmin presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, the chairman reported that Mr. Zhu Zhixin had a long history in the National Revolution. During the war to protect the constitution, when the Gui rebels occupied Guangdong, Mr. Zhu Zhixin traveled between Hong Kong and Shanghai to negotiate military affairs with great effort. Unfortunately, he was killed in Humen in 1920. Looking back on Mr. Zhu's great life, what the comrades of our party should emulate is: 1. He had special intelligence and could read several lines at a glance. After a little research on Chinese and foreign studies, he had his own insights. His writings were extremely profound and exquisite, and he could write ten thousand words in a single sitting, as if he had prepared them in advance. His diligent pursuit of knowledge, frugality, and steadfastness were especially beyond what ordinary people could achieve. 2. As a scholarly general, he led more than 100,000 troops and made decisive decisions when things happened. He was brave based on righteousness to be loyal to his beliefs, and his outlook on life was extremely indifferent, without considering personal interests or asking about power and glory. He once did not hesitate to demote himself to the position of accounting director to clean up Guangdong's finances. 3. He had a well-trained spirit, and although he often faced life and death, his courage was extraordinary. He never wavered. He had a great deal of research on military affairs, and his article "The Psychology of Soldiers and Its Transformation" was praised by Chiang Kai-shek. All of the above are manifestations of Mr. Zhu's great spirit throughout his life. We should emulate the martyrs to be worthy of the meaning of the commemoration. Chen Bulei then delivered a speech saying that he deeply admired Mr. Zhu's personality, learning, writing, and strategy, and at the same time, he felt that our comrades should especially emulate his integrity and magnanimity in believing in Mr. Zhu. Now that China is in such a difficult situation, young people's thoughts are so complicated, and society is becoming increasingly precarious, all because people in general have lost their cultivation in integrity and magnanimity. In the future, we should actively promote morality and pay attention to cultivation in order to correct social evils. The meeting adjourned after the speech.

Hunan-Jiangxi Troops Surround and Suppress the Communist Bandits

Hunan Army's Four Divisions Pursue in Two Routes

He Jian Cables Situation of Bandits' Flight

Changsha Communication: After the failure of the Communist bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, Lin (Biao), Kong (Hechong), Li (Shixing), etc. to invade the province with all their forces, they initially planned to flee to Jiangxi via Liling to attack Ji'an. If they could not enter Jiangxi, they would directly take Xiangnan via Caiyou. However, Peng and Huang had differing opinions with Zhu and Mao. Peng and Huang believed that gathering in one place would risk encirclement by the National Army. They advocated dividing into smaller groups to harass Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, thereby dispersing the National Army's forces and preventing them from concentrating on suppression. They also wanted Zhu, Mao, etc. to carry out their initial plan to flee to Jiangxi, while Peng, Huang, etc. would temporarily return to their old nests in Liuping to seize opportunities to harass Hunan and Hubei again. Zhu and Mao initially opposed, but Peng and Huang had greater influence and the ability to sway the Communist bandits. Since Peng and Huang insisted, they finally implemented their plan. Currently, the majority of Zhu and Mao's forces have crossed Liling and are advancing rapidly towards Pingxiang. The majority of Peng and Huang's forces have retreated to Liuyang County and are building defensive works at Jiaoxi Ridge in an attempt to resist stubbornly. He Jian has now assigned four divisions, divided into two routes, to pursue. On the Jiangxi front, when the Communist bandits made their general retreat on the 13th and 14th, He Jian immediately telegraphed Lu Dipin, requesting him to send troops to block them as soon as possible. Yesterday, he received Lu's reply, stating that he had already ordered Zhang Huizan's division to leave Pingxiang and block Zhu and Mao towards Liling, and Tan Daoyuan's division to leave Wanzai and block Peng and Huang towards Liuyang. Thus, the Communist bandits are now trapped in an encirclement by the armies of Hunan and Jiangxi provinces.

The situation of the Communist bandits' retreat, according to aerial reconnaissance reports, is as follows: On the 18th, at 7:00 AM, squadron leader Zhang Yuheng and navigator Yang Xialin, aboard Dallas No. 1 aircraft, inspected the situation in Liling, You County, Anren, and the suburbs of the provincial capital. (A) On the right flank: 1. On the railway in Wulipai, west of Liling, there were about 1,000 bandits with guns. Three heavy bombs were dropped and 100 machine gun rounds were fired, killing many bandits. On the northern bank of the iron bridge to the east, there were hundreds of bandits with spears marching towards Liling. To the south, the figures in Sifen were chaotic, making it difficult to distinguish between civilians and bandits. In Youtangpu, bordering Pingxiang to the east, and on the small roads on both sides of the shop, there were scattered bandits advancing towards Pingxiang. 2. Luko is still occupied by bandits, with more than 40 large civilian boats and more than 10 rafts moored on the riverbank. On the small road east of the city, there were scattered bandits marching towards the city. 3. There were no traces of bandits in You County, Anren, Zhuzhou, Shiwan, Zhaoling, and Zhuting. However, there were scattered groups of three to five bandits marching towards Luko on the small paths in Zhuzhou. 4. In Huangtuling, You County, there were about 40,000 bandits with spears gathered in one place. A speaking platform was erected there, seemingly for a meeting. The aircraft descended and fired 300 machine gun rounds, seeing the bandits fleeing in panic and disorder, with corpses strewn along the way. (B) On the left flank: 1. There were about 400 bandits with guns between Jintang and Dadu, marching towards Zhentou Town. Three bombs were dropped. There were no traces of bandits east of Zhentou Town. However, there were many people in Pujishi, seemingly bandits hiding. Four bombs were dropped, killing countless people. 2. The government troops stationed in Dongshan and Langlishi are advancing towards Yongan City and Jiaoxi Ridge. Yesterday, He Jian telegraphed all armies and county militias to strictly guard against the Communist bandits. The record is as follows: (Titles omitted) The bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, etc., after their repeated general offensive on Changsha from Zhengwan, fiercely attacked our army with tens of thousands of troops. They fell forward and followed each other twice, but were finally overwhelmed by our firepower, and their deaths were countless. Yesterday morning, they were bombed by our artillery and aircraft, making them even more unable to support themselves. Therefore, starting from Yuan morning, Zhu Mao's faction retreated towards Zhuli. Their vanguard arrived at Licheng on Hanshen, appearing to flee east to Pingxiang. Peng Huang's faction was still entrenched in Yijiawan and Tiaomajian on Hanri. They began moving east on Shan morning, appearing to be fleeing to Liuyang again. Our army is currently following and pursuing them. We will arrive at Jintuo, Gongsigang, Tiaomajian, and Tianxinqiao on Xianri. The provincial capital has entered a state of complete peace and tranquility. It is found that the retreat of the bandits this time is indeed due to excessive damage and internal discord, so their actions are extremely embarrassing. Now the Central Army has dispatched a large army on the way, and the Jiangxi army has also dispatched troops to attack from the east and west, and it is not difficult to annihilate them. However, the bandits' usual trick is to divide into smaller groups after defeat, or flee or lie dormant, in order to plot secret growth and potential harm. If no measures are taken to eliminate them, it will be a hidden danger in the future. Our local garrison militias have considerable strength. Since they know that they have suffered heavy losses, they should take this opportunity to calmly deploy, strictly defend and suppress, and investigate and arrest them, so that they will not flee into or hide in the territory, and eliminate future troubles forever. A telegram is urgently issued and investigated and acted upon. Commander He Jian. Qiaohai Printed (September 18th).

Wuhan's Martial Law Remains Strict

No Vessels Allowed on the River After 12 PM

Citywide Inspections Conducted at Random Times and Locations

Hankou Communication: The Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, in order to consolidate public security, will request the Wuhan Commander-in-Chief's headquarters to prohibit ships from traveling at night and to conduct inspections at random times, locations, and frequencies from the 22nd to prevent Communist bandits from hiding. After receiving the request, the Commander-in-Chief's headquarters, in addition to ordering Navy Commander Zeng Yiding to strictly enforce it, also ordered the Hankou Municipal Government to notify the consuls of various countries to inform foreign ships. The inspections will be directly handled by the Garrison Department, which has issued a notice to the public to avoid misunderstandings. The letter from the Municipal Government to the consuls in Hankou is as follows: Dear Sirs, We have recently received a telegram from the Acting Commander-in-Chief's headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, stating that Wuhan Garrison Commander Xia Douyin reported that the 22nd meeting of the Hankou Martial Law Commander, the commander of the 3rd Gendarmerie Regiment Ouyang Zhen, proposed that if friendly forces' troops arrive in Wuhan at night by ship, our garrison troops will easily cause misunderstandings by refusing to allow them to land. If they are allowed to pass, accidents may occur. What should be done? After full discussion, it was decided that since the three cities of Wuhan were placed under martial law by the order of the Ministry on August 1st, land and water traffic have been cut off after 12:00 PM. However, on the water surface, troop transport ships still forcibly enter the area after 12:00 PM, making it impossible to check or stop them. Now that the Communist bandits are rampant and rebellious, the river defense is as important as the land defense. A slight carelessness will lead to great disasters. In order to prevent traitors and avoid misunderstandings with friendly forces, the department has submitted a document to the Ministry, requesting the Ministry to order two warships to be stationed, one in the middle of the river at Baishazhou and one in the middle of the river at Chenjiaji. According to the land method, traffic will be completely cut off from 12:00 PM to 5:00 AM the next morning. During this time, if any troop transport ships enter the garrison area on the river, the warships will block them and report to the Ministry for instructions on whether to allow them to enter. The Ministry will then notify the department by telephone, and the department will notify the garrison troops and agencies by telephone. Otherwise, they will not be allowed to enter to ensure confidentiality and avoid misunderstandings. The record is on file. Is this appropriate? We hereby submit a document to Your Excellency for review, and we request your instructions to comply with it for the public convenience. In addition to ordering the department to notify the Water Police Bureau to send two small boats under the command of Commander Zeng Yiding and to order sailors to assist on the small boats, please also inform the consuls of various countries stationed in Hankou to notify the shipping companies of their respective countries not to allow their ships to enter the garrison area after 12:00 PM and before 5:00 AM the next morning. Apart from separating one

Page 10

letter, we hereby send this letter to Your Excellency the Consul for your review and to inform the shipping companies of various countries to comply with it. Sincerely yours (September 20th).

Internal Division in Lu Xingbang's Forces

Lu's Troops Withdraw from Yan, Jian, and Shao Prefectures

Fuzhou Communication: Lu Xingbang took the initiative to retreat and shorten his defensive line because the provincial army was attacking from Yongchun, Shouning, and Fuzhou in three directions. Zhou Zhiqin's brigade was originally cooperating with Lu Xingbang and his brother Xingrong, but now he has pledged allegiance to the provincial government. Chen Rongbiao's regiment has a historical relationship with Lu's division. However, the Lu brothers, considering Chen's two surrenders to Wang Yongquan and Zhou Yinren leading the Northern Army to attack Fujian as a danger to their hearts, plotted to deal with him. On the one hand, they promoted Chen to the commander of the supplementary brigade to show restraint. On the other hand, they transferred one regiment of his troops to Dahu and one regiment to Gutian, secretly monitored by Lu Xingrong and Lu's regiment commander Qian Yuguang, in order to resolve Chen at an opportune time. Chen did not take it seriously, as the elite troops of Lu's forces were in his hands. However, Chen usually competed with Qian Yuguang in Gutian for compiling bandits and distributing salaries, with a disdain for everything. Qian could not bear it and believed that he had to remove Chen at the right opportunity. Recently, Lu Xingrong newly appointed his nephew Chen Guanlu as the magistrate of Gutian County. Qian then conspired with Chen to set up a banquet in Mingluntang on September 3rd, inviting Chen to drink. Ambush soldiers were placed on both sides, and he was arrested and killed after half a drink. When one regiment of Chen's troops stationed in Gu heard the news, they rioted and looted in the town and countryside. Qian's regiment was unable to stop them due to its weak strength, so they had to allow them to carry weapons up the mountain. When Lu Xingrong received Qian Yuguang's telegram about one regiment of Chen's troops in Dahu, he immediately sent a team to surround and disarm them. After a fierce battle for half a day, half of Chen's troops escaped.

Lu's forces have become weaker after this incident. In addition, they have been trapped in northern Fujian for a long time and are experiencing extreme difficulties in supply. Knowing that prolonged stalemate is not a good solution, Lu Xingbang and Lu Xingrong retreated on their own and handed over their troops to Lu Xingming. Lu Xingrong was arrested and taken to the provincial government on January 6th of this year, after which he went to Shanghai and did not ask about military affairs due to disagreement with the government. He expressed dissatisfaction with this war, so he was greatly understood by Yang Shuzhuang. Currently, Lu's forces have withdrawn from Yan, Jian, and Shao prefectures and are temporarily stationed in Youxi, Shaxian, Yongan, Dehua, and Datian counties, awaiting reorganization by the central government. Therefore, there are no Lu's troops in the western suburbs of the provincial capital recently. The provincial capital announced the lifting of special martial law from the 11th of this month, and inspections are not as strict as before (September 12th).

Fuzhou Business Guilds Request Exemption from Apportionment

Fuzhou Communication: The various business guilds have recently been strictly apportioned a loan of 500,000 yuan by the Finance Department, so they have submitted petitions to various agencies requesting relief from business difficulties. The text of the petition is as follows: We petition for the extreme difficulty of business, requesting a transfer to the Finance Department to stop the loan process in order to relieve business difficulties. The reason is that the Finance Department has apportioned a loan of 500,000 yuan to the various business guilds. The business guilds have stated their difficulties and requested exemption, but this has not been examined, and the Finance Department has proceeded strictly according to its own will. The business guilds have no way to advance or retreat and have to cry bitterly to your association. Fuzhou is the center of the province, but it is neither a commercial production area nor a commercial sales market, but only a transportation hub for upstream and downstream. In recent years, there have been almost no peaceful days due to bandits and wars upstream and downstream. The commerce of the provincial capital has long since declined. In addition, the citywide road construction last year caused the business to stop and the construction required huge expenses. All businessmen were exhausted. Before the wounds were healed, the military affairs of Tao Lu arose again. The streams and rivers were cut off, and the whole city was in turmoil. Bills of exchange were delayed and the delivery dates were stopped. The businessmen themselves had nowhere to borrow money, let alone borrow from others. If it is said that there is borrowing and repayment, then the merchant is not donating. If the merchant has cash, bills of exchange can be cashed, and delivery dates can be arranged. However, even the most important problem is forced to sit and become a stalemate. Even if there are extremely credible pledges and extremely rich funds, there is no money to borrow. How can the Finance Department Chief see such a tragic situation of the merchants and immediately impose an apportionment upon arriving? It seems that it does not conform to the Three Principles of the People. Now, the business guilds believe that they have no power to borrow for self-defense, and they have no power. They can only present the difficulties and request your association to uphold justice and quickly transfer to the Finance Department to stop the loan to the business guilds in order to relieve business difficulties. We are grateful for your kindness.

In addition to the 80,000 yuan for the Qian Guild, which has been agreed upon, the Finance Department has set 150,000 yuan for the Tea and Wood Guilds, and the other guilds are also being agreed upon by the department for a quota of 150,000 yuan. The detailed numbers are as follows: 30,000 yuan for paper and stream, 30,000 yuan for silk and cloth, 16,000 yuan for pawn, 4,000 yuan for pine wood, 8,000 yuan for medicinal materials, 7,600 yuan for cotton yarn, 400 yuan for copy shop, 1,200 yuan for city sauce garden, 1,200 yuan for Taiwan sauce garden, 600 yuan for wine and rice, 400 yuan for stream rice, 280 yuan for Wubei rice, 1,600 yuan for tobacco leaves, 3,600 yuan for cotton ramie and water tobacco, 360 yuan for city Su and Guang, 600 yuan for Taiwan Su and Guang, 560 yuan for paint, 1,000 yuan for fresh fish, 1,000 yuan for salted fish, 600 yuan for Xiaoshandong, 6,254 yuan for wine, 1,040 yuan for iron, 2,000 yuan for gold, 660 yuan for pearls, 600 yuan for porcelain, 800 yuan for silk thread, 1,100 yuan for raw lacquer, 800 yuan for bean guild, 320 yuan for fruits, 600 yuan for fresh flowers, 600 yuan for miscellaneous boards, 740 yuan for city money style, 1,252 yuan for straight road money style, 1,120 yuan for horizontal road money style, 600 yuan for Qiaonan money style, 400 yuan for oil, 4,360 yuan for powder, 6,200 yuan for sea transportation, 4,000 yuan for passengers, 400 yuan for customs declaration, and 4,000 yuan for passenger wine. In recent days, the department has sent members Fang Yingtuan and Zheng Shupeng to directly urge the various commercial firms, but the merchants still find it difficult to accept.

Nanning Still Under Siege

Guangxi Army Flees to Hunan Border via Fuhe

Guangdong Supplies Yunnan Army with Ammunition to Attack Yong

Guangzhou Communication: In the Guangxi province war, the Guilin army has recently moved around the area of ​​PingLe Longhu Pass. Zhang Fakui and Tang Shengming, etc. have also moved all troops out of the border of Guilin. Recently, the situation on the Fuhe side suddenly became tense. It is said that the Guilin army used newly compiled teams to deliberately advance into the area of ​​PingLe Zhaoping, so as to cover the retreat of their main force through Longhu Pass to the border of Hunan. Now most of them have crossed the border. All the new soldiers stationed in Zhaoping have returned to PingLe, and the garrison teams of Zhou Guozhi and Su Meisen, which were stationed in PingLe, have also retreated to Yangshuo a week ago. Xue Pingqing's troops stationed in Mengshan also retreated to Guilin on the 10th and took away the guns and equipment of the local militia. The newly compiled division of Huang Mingyuan, stationed in Xiuren Lipu, also retreated to Guilin on the same day. At present, from PingLe to Xiuren Lipu, there are only two militia teams stationed. The Guangxi Security Commander of the Eighth Route Army, Lu Dingxiang, believes that the enemy is retreating step by step and can take the opportunity to pursue. He specially sent a telegram from the front to ask for a strategy. The telegram said that it was reported that the rebel army stationed in Ping had fled to Yangshuo, and more than a hundred remnants of the rebel army stationed in Meng had fled to Guilin. All the counties of Pingzhao, Li, and Xiu were empty. The telegram was sent to the headquarters on Wen day to order friendly forces along the river to take all the counties. The telegram arrived, please ask the two staff officers to ask for instructions nearby and plan everything for the counterattack (omitted below). Dingxiang叩Yuan Chenyinyunyun The Guangxi army of Fuhe has retreated to the border of Hunan, and the exact report of its actions is not yet available. The northern Guangdong borders southern Hunan, and the Eighth Route Army has drawn a considerable force to defend the northwest Jiangxi. The Guangxi side is guarded by the Yu Hanmou and Li Yangjing divisions and Huang Renhuan brigade to guard the Fu and Da rivers. The Nanning side is still under siege. The Eighth Route Army sent an air force and warships to assist the Yunnan army in the siege. Now airplanes fly to Yongyuan every day to drop bombs, and the Fourth Fleet sent Haiou, Jiangda, Jiangshun, Pingxi, Xinsongjiang, and Lichen and other shallow-water ships to Yongchun River to assist in the attack on Yongcheng South Gate. Lu Han's Yunnan Army's 99th Division Zhu Xu's troops have been transferred from Wuming to attack Yong, only leaving the 3rd Brigade Sun Du's troops stationed in Wu to contact the Eighth Route Army Yu Division. It is planned that the first batch transferred from Qinzhou, Nanlu will be handed over to the Yunnan Army Zhang Chong Division Long Tuan to transport into Guilin. The second batch will be transported by the Hairui ship to Qinlian for inventory, totaling more than 70 boxes of ammunition. In recent days, after the Yunnan Army received ammunition, the attack on Yong was very urgent. At present, Nanning is under siege, and the Guilin army has been trapped for more than a month, and the ammunition is exhausted. The residents in the city are even more miserable. The traffic is blocked, and everything is expensive. The water for drinking costs several yuan per burden. It is conceivable that other prices are expensive. Moreover, airplanes arrive to drop bombs every day, and the residents have no defenses. Often, a bomb is dropped, and several members of the family are buried in the smoke and gunpowder. Therefore, they all hope that the Guilin army will leave as soon as possible, so that the military affairs can be resolved (September 17th).

Recent Financial Situation of Guangdong Province

Monthly Military Expenses Still Amount to 4.2 Million, National Treasury Loans No Less Than 31 Million

Guangzhou Communication: Since the start of the military campaign in Guangdong Province, military expenses have consistently been above 4 million yuan per month, resulting in monthly administrative expenses being in arrears. The authorities are currently planning to set monthly military expenses at 4.2 million yuan and will not increase them any further. According to financial circles, the reason for the recent financial difficulties of the provincial treasury is entirely due to loans from the national treasury for military use. The provincial treasury is managed by the Department of Finance, while the national treasury is managed by the Finance Special Commissioner's Office, and the funds borrowed from the provincial treasury are all transferred by the national treasury for military salaries. It is found that from March of last year to August 15 of this year, the national treasury borrowed no less than 31.1 million yuan from the provincial treasury. If the military affairs cannot be ended in the future, the provincial treasury will continue to bear military expenses and loans of 1.7 to 1.8 million yuan per month. This large amount of expenses will not only affect the provincial administrative expenses from being paid on schedule, but also make it impossible to increase the education and construction expenses. Therefore, when the Yunnan Army representatives came to Guangdong to request military pay, the authorities politely declined because the military expenses were beyond the budget and introduced the Yunnan representatives to the central government to request direct supply from the National Government. Recently, the financial treasury bonds issued here have been sold in succession. According to statistics yesterday, as of mid-September, the total amount of bonds sold by the General Chamber of Commerce was 600,000, of which 200,000 have been sold; the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau was 850,000, of which 270,000 have been sold; the Shantou Branch Gold Treasury was originally set at 700,000 and 850,000 have been issued first; Beihai 40,000, Haikou Port 300,000, Jiangmen City 250,000, Shaozhou 200,000. In addition, the total amount directly purchased from the Department of Finance by various contractors and received by various counties was 3.4 million yuan. The total amount of funds returned by various agencies and contractors after underwriting was about 1.2 million yuan, of which half was paper and half was silver. The funds received were handed over to the Central Bank as a fund, which has been done four times: the first time was 68,000, the second time was 192,000, the third time was 134,000, and the fourth time was 60,000. The total amount deposited in the Central Bank was 454,000 yuan. The reason why various parties promoted the sale of treasury bonds this time was that a part of it stipulated that those who purchased it in the first month could receive half of the uncashed paper money, so before September 15, the citizens searched for uncashed paper money to pay rent and taxes. Therefore, the price of uncashed paper money has been higher than before. The price of uncashed five-yuan and ten-yuan bills from the Central Bank has risen to 86-87% in recent days. It is heard that the Central Bank is preparing to choose one of the above two types of bills and restore the exchange as soon as the finances are slightly active. The mill currency recasting factory under the jurisdiction of the Department of Finance has been closed for a long time. Until recently, it suddenly announced that Xu Xiqing was the director of the mill currency factory (Xu was the former mayor of Shantou). Xu took over the job on the 11th. He is currently actively repairing the machinery in the factory. According to Xu, the Department of Finance specially restored the mill currency factory to cast coins in order to circulate finances. Many Hong Kong dollars have been collected in advance for the purchase of raw silver, so the exchange rate of Hong Kong dollars has risen from 305 to 321, which has no impact on the government. Since the factory is preparing raw silver, it can start casting around September 20. He is currently looking for workers to sort out the machinery and prepare everything (September 15th).

Ning-Shao Association in Songjiang Established: The Ning-Shao natives in Songjiang are planning to establish a hometown association. They have already recruited more than 500 members. Lawyers Association Regularly Reviews Member Qualifications: The Songjiang Lawyers Association held a council meeting the day before yesterday and decided that members who join the association must fill out a membership application form and submit their diploma certificates to the association. Wuxi

County and District Associations Strive to Retain the County Add-on Grain Tax: The Jiangsu Provincial County Agricultural, Forestry, and Sericulture Field Association, in view of the Finance Department's clear text order to add two yuan per stone to the county's grain tax, referred to the precedent and sent a letter to the county and district associations yesterday to jointly strive with the construction, education, and other bureaus to retain five corners for county use to fund local undertakings. The original letter is recorded below: We hereby inform you that the counties of our province have received the Finance Department's order to add two yuan per stone to the grain tax according to the precedent of the 16th year. However, the previous plan had five corners per stone retained for county use as an eleven-point distribution for local undertakings, with the agricultural, forestry, and sericulture field accounting for two-tenths and five-hundredths. Now that the grain tax has been added, there is no clear text to retain five corners for county use. At this time when collection is about to begin, all local agencies should strive to retain five corners for county use in order to fund local undertakings.

Two Water and Land Robberies in One Day: There are three regular shipping routes between the local area and Suzhou. The day before yesterday, the third shipping route loaded goods in Wuxi and set off for Suzhou. At about 2:00 AM that night, it passed through the Xiaoshendu area of Xin'an Township and suddenly encountered a pirate ship. More than a dozen pirates jumped onto the ship with guns and searched extensively. It is estimated that they robbed more than 80 yuan in cash and summer cloth, with a total loss of more than 700 yuan. In addition, Shao Xiuhua, a villager in Shibu, Kaiyuan Township, Fourth District (Kaiyuan Township), was robbed by seven or eight bandits who broke into his house the night before last, with a total loss of several hundred yuan. Wang Shikui's family, Shao's eastern neighbor, was also robbed and searched, and Wang's father-in-law, Bei Huanquan, was held and beaten. Yesterday, the victim Shao Xiuhua and others reported to the Ninth Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau, which was forwarded to the County Public Security Bureau for instructions to assist in the arrest.

Anti-Smuggling Team Repels Salt Smugglers: On the 20th night, there were 40 to 50 salt smugglers wantonly harassing the Wangting North Bridge area of the 13th District. After hearing the news, the 7th Anti-Smuggling Brigade immediately led a team to suppress them. After two hours of fierce fighting, the bandits were unable to support themselves and retreated, fleeing into the surrounding villages. In this battle, one water police officer was shot and injured, and a certain patrol officer's right eye was injured. He was immediately ordered to be sent to Puren Hospital in the city for treatment by ambulance.

Changzhou

Xueyan Bridge Detects Bandit Ship: Xueyan Bridge Town, Wuyi, is located on the edge of Taihu Lake and is a place where bandits often appear. Recently, Mao District Chief, the second district chief of the water police stationed in Wuxi, sent a warship to guard it. On the evening of the 19th, soldiers detected a bandit. Then, Wu Zongjie, the town's security team leader, led the team and detected another bandit ship, arrested two bandits, Ma Hongchu and Hang Heshang, and seized a live pistol. After interrogation, they were found to be related to the Yixi robbery case and were scheduled to be sent to the county for interrogation within a few days.

Liu District Chief's Murder Case Acquitted: Liu Baorun, the former district chief of the Fourth District of Wuyi, was previously accused of murder in the bandit suppression case and was transferred to the County Court Inspection Office for investigation and prosecution. He has been detained for a long time. After a public trial, the verdict was scheduled to be announced on the 20th. Yesterday, Judge Xue Chongguang appeared in court to read out the text of the judgment, stating that Liu Baorun was acquitted of the murder charge. After the verdict was announced, Liu Baorun was ordered to be returned to custody.

Zhenjiang

Passenger Robbed on Boat: Old Zhou New Bridge Town Resident of Jiangbei, Shu Fanggui, was traveling across the river on the 11th Red Boat yesterday. When the boat reached the center of the river, bandits demanded 300 yuan from Shu. Shu ignored them, and they began to beat him. Shu, having no money on the boat, said he would find a way after reaching town. The accomplices of the bandit on the boat, including Wang Decai, Wang Xinbao, Wang Guiben, Xu Sheng, and Wang Ziliang, monitored him. After the boat reached town, they stayed at the Zhonghua Hotel together. Shu then managed to hand over 140 silver dollars. Wang Decai, after receiving the money, released Shu, who then went to the court and public safety bureau to report the incident. The detective team rushed to arrest the bandits, but the ringleader has not yet been captured.

Thorough Investigation of the Shady Dealings of the Mongolian Relief Institute: Chen Tianmin, a member of the Second District, Second Branch of the party, stated that the Mongolian Relief Institute has been plagued by problems for years. Every year, it requests 2,000 yuan from the province, all of which is embezzled and divided among accomplices, and no relief is distributed. He had previously submitted a request to the county party headquarters, which was forwarded to the provincial party headquarters, requesting the provincial government to order the county government and the Small Benevolence Relief Institute to thoroughly investigate the institute. The institute has refused to hand over the account books for the past years and has not provided clear explanations for the suspicious points. Yesterday, he again proposed at the 23rd party member meeting of the Second District, Second Branch, to forward the request again for a swift investigation.

Seizure of a Privately Recruited Band of Bandits: Ma Shan, suspected to be from Zhenjiang, lived at No. 10 Minguo Spring Street outside the city. He went to Hankou a month ago to seek employment with Commander Fan Shisheng but failed. Later, he falsely recruited a band of bandits. Commander Fan discovered this and immediately reported it to He Yingqin, the chief of the military affairs department, who ordered his arrest. He also telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering a thorough investigation of Ma's residence. After receiving the telegram, the provincial government ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to instruct the Provincial Public Safety Bureau to comply. The bureau, led by Inspector Xu Yuyin and Officer Wang of the Fifth Precinct, along with many senior police officers, went to No. 10 Minguo Spring Street yesterday to search the premises. They found box guns, bullets, and other items. Ma Shan's suspected wife was also taken to the bureau for questioning.

Yangzhou

Private Smuggling of Silver Dollars: Complete Release. The Public Safety Bureau's First Precinct seized twenty carts of privately smuggled silver dollars. The bureau has now handed the case over to the county, and yesterday (19th) they were completely released. Public opinion is in an uproar. The county government issued a notice publicizing the name of the smuggler to quell the rumors. It is said that the Chamber of Commerce, based on a report from the Money Trade Association, stated to the county that the silver dollars were for purchasing goods or domestic circulation and were not being smuggled out of the country.

Nantong

Construction of Coastal Military Road: Coastal areas and fields are plagued by rampant pirates. The salt, reclamation, and planting industries suffer the greatest losses. Military police have difficulty suppressing them due to obstructed transportation. Recently, a large group of pirates has fled to Yancheng and Funing. Military police have divided the area for defense and are working with the police to build a coastal military road, starting with the section from Beixing Bridge to Erjia, and utilizing the existing Fan Gong embankment to reach Yancheng and Funing.

Large Quantities of Arms and Ammunition Transported from Shanghai to Nantong: Banditary is rampant in Nantong County. Various districts are actively organizing self-defense groups. The county government has obtained approval from the provincial and central governments to purchase 500 rifles, 300 box guns, 50 Thompson submachine guns, and 100,000 rounds of ammunition, which will be transported in batches from Shanghai for use.

Recruiting Soldiers Despite Civilian Fear and Prohibition: Cao, the director of the 31st Rear Hospital, recently sent letters to various county governments to prohibit the recruitment of recovered soldiers from Tong and the surrounding areas by civilian groups, as many soldiers have been recruited.

Rugao

Large Number of Suspicious Monks Arrested and Detained: The Juegang District Office of Rugao, under orders, joined forces with the Fengma and Ju districts to search for bandits in the border area. They arrested more than 20 suspicious monks, one tailor, one cook, and seized opium, bullets, dice, etc. at the Xu Guanyin Temple, Shuanghui Mountain, Wangjiatan, and other places. More than ten people were taken to Matang, and the rest were detained at the Juegang District Office. The district office sent them to the county government for interrogation on the 16th. The county government opened a court for interrogation yesterday (17th). Those who appeared in court included Zeng Weian, Yuanyuan, Jiyuan, Tuolun, Hailiang, Guoli, etc. According to the monks, they were not bandits, and they did not know where the bullets came from. The opium was used to help residents quit opium and avoid morphine injections. The dice were for young monks to play with. The tailor, Jin Sheng, said that he was a tailor and was arrested for making clothes for the monks at the temple. The cook, Jiang Liancheng, said that none of the monks in the temple had joined the Communist Party or colluded with bandits. The abbot, Zeng Weifeng, and the monks gave similar accounts. Zhu, the presiding judge, ordered six monks, including Zeng Weifeng, to be detained for investigation, and Jin Sheng and Jiang Liancheng were released on bail.

Hangzhou

High Court Handles Prison Break Case: The Zhejiang Higher Court, regarding the serious prison break in Fenghua County, where one person was killed and five were recaptured, but the remaining 68 escapees were all robbers and major criminals, immediately telegraphed all levels of courts and distributed the case to various city and county governments, military and police agencies for joint arrest. The prison warden, Hong Jinqi, was dismissed from his post and sent to the province for interrogation. His vacancy was filled by Du Guiqing.

Appointment and Transfer of Financial Officials in Various Counties: Qian Yongming, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance, stated that Director Chen of the Changkai Donation Bureau was not handling matters well and has been transferred to the province to await reassignment. Huang Qingzhong will fill the vacancy. In addition, Zheng Jun, Director of the Linhai Finance Bureau, resigned with approval. Zhang Zhengfan will fill the vacancy. Furthermore, Zhang Kaidi, Chief of the Third Section of the Department, has repeatedly requested to resign due to illness, and his vacancy has also been filled by Liang Junren.

Shaoxing

County Magistrate and Chamber of Commerce Raise Funds for Security Corps: The Shaoxing Security Corps requires approximately 36,000 yuan per year, but there is no designated source of funds, making it extremely difficult to operate. A meeting has been held to decide on a method, modeled after the cases of Xinchang and Shengxian counties, to levy an additional four jiao per tael of land tax, which would yield 24,000 yuan. The remaining one-third, or 12,000 yuan, will be subsidized by merchants, with the shop tax as the standard for collection. In addition to submitting a request to the province for approval, the county magistrate and the county chamber of commerce will follow the plan to raise funds.

Xiaoshan

Robbery Occurs in Shanshanquan: A Longchang small goods store in Zhengjia Alley in Shanshanquan outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan was broken into by five or six robbers on the night of the 17th. They knocked on the door and entered. A shop assistant happened to be there, and a robber immediately fired a pistol, hitting a vital spot. The assistant fell to the ground in pain. Fortunately, another assistant escaped through the back door and notified the neighbors, who beat gongs. The robbers only took several tens of dollars from the desk and left. It is reported that the injured assistant died the next morning due to severe injuries. The shop owner immediately reported the incident to the Suoqian Public Safety Bureau, ordering a strict arrest. The Water Patrol Team's Prolonged Detention of Ships is Accused: The Xiaoshan Jiangsi is stationed in the inland river police force, which this time because there is a Keiqiao opened to Xixing night cruise ship was detained for more than twenty days, illegally detained boaters pass sixty-one case. It is heard that the shipping industry believes that the team's arbitrary detention of ships is illegal, and has separately presented the case to the provincial government and the general headquarters, requesting an investigation and verification.

Mingguang

Department Order Thorough Investigation of Public Safety Bureau Chief: Wang Lianju, the head of the Mingguang Public Safety Bureau, was previously accused by the Fifth District Party Department, District Office, Chamber of Commerce, and other agencies to the Department of Civil Affairs of smoking opium, harboring opium traffickers, and creating litigation malpractices. The Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county government to investigate and reply. County Magistrate Tang has dispatched Administrative Committee Member Feng Ziyi to conduct a thorough investigation.

The Municipal Education Bureau has received instructions from the Ministry of Education that the song and dance dramas performed by elementary schools during游藝 fairs are not in line with educational principles and are detrimental to the physical and mental health of children. Municipal Education Bureau Orders

Private Schools to Apply for Registration by a Deadline

Those that do not meet the standards will be strictly shut down

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued an order to all unregistered private schools at all levels, stating that the Ministry of Education's order No. 932 stated that there are many private schools of varying quality in Shanghai and that they should all be registered as soon as possible for the purpose of reorganization. According to the bureau's report, the schools are often hesitant to register. The ministry instructed that those that do not meet the standards should be shut down according to law. However, recent reports indicate that unregistered private schools in Shanghai are still advertising for enrollment and creating various titles to exaggerate and attract attention. Their advertising shows that they are focused on profit and disregard reality. The bureau should select those that meet the agreed standards and urge them to register quickly, and strictly shut down those that do not meet the standards to avoid misleading young people and hindering education. The bureau has repeatedly issued notices urging private schools to comply with the regulations and register, and has sent personnel to supervise them. However, many unregistered schools still remain. In accordance with the previous order, in addition to thoroughly investigating and strictly shutting down all schools that do not meet the standards, all schools should be urged to comply with the regulations and apply for registration as soon as possible. Those that fail to comply will be deemed to have acknowledged that they do not meet the standards. The bureau will comply with the ministry's order to shut down those that do not meet the standards.

The Chinese Vocational Guidance

Agencies Joint Association Established Yesterday

Passed Constitution and Established Executive Committee

General Assembly to be Held in the Capital in December

Permanent Mailing Address: Chinese Vocational Education Society

The Chinese Vocational Guidance Agencies Joint Association held its founding meeting yesterday at the Chinese Vocational Education Society. More than sixty representatives from fifty agencies and organizations attended. Liu Zhanen chaired the meeting, and Wang Jianhou recorded the proceedings. After the usual formalities, the chairman delivered the opening address, followed by Jiang Wenyu, representing the Vocational Education Society, who gave a welcoming speech. Yang Weiyu then reported on the recent activities of the Vocational Education Society, and Pan Yangyao reported on the preparations for the association. He Qingru, Shen Yougan, and Chen Xuanshan delivered speeches. The meeting then discussed the agenda and adjourned. Afterwards, a tea party was held on the roof of the Vocational Education Society, followed by a banquet for the representatives. The details of the meeting are recorded below.

Attendees: Zhu Hange of the Shanghai County Education Bureau, Li Yizhi of the Patriotic Girls' Middle School, Wu Xixu and Wang Xingchi of the Wuxian Vocational Guidance Center, Wang Zemin of the Jiangsu Provincial Suzhou Girls' Middle School, Xu Zihua of the Yixing County Education Bureau, Fei Dasheng of the Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture School, Cao Cishan of the Nantong County Education Bureau, Rui Ziyu of the Jiangsu Provincial Wuxi Middle School, Zhang Zhongbao of the Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School, Wang Fumin of the Puyi Society Vocational Introduction Department, Gu Wenwei of the Minli Middle School, Cheng Kuanzheng of the Wusong Middle School, Yang Chongya of the Tongji University, Niu Changyao of the Jingye Middle School, Xie Yicheng of the Nanjing Municipal Vocational Guidance Center, Shen Hongchen of the National Central University, Yu Shoumei of the Jiangsu Provincial Education College, Li Yongzhen and Chen Junren of the Nantong University Agricultural Science Department, Liu Zhanen of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, Bao Yuqi of the Guanghua University, Chen Xuanshan of the Datong University, Shen Wenmei of the Suzhou Middle School, Pan Yangyao of the Chinese Vocational School, Ding Yuan of the Shanghai Meiwei College, Xi Junyu of the Hujiang University, Yang Zhuofu of the Jiading County Education Bureau, etc.

Summary of Speeches: Chairman Liu Zhanen's opening address stated that vocational guidance requires impartiality. If impartiality is emphasized, there is no need for vocational guidance. Most of China is currently unemployed, and even those who are employed are often unable to settle down and enjoy their work. Recognizing this, the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center was established. The National Education Conference had important proposals and resolutions regarding vocational guidance. Now, universities, middle schools, and educational institutions across the country are establishing vocational guidance agencies. However, how to connect, research, and implement these agencies effectively requires the joint efforts of comrades in various regions. This is the reason for today's meeting. The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center has been established for two years, and its mission is very important. The education community can easily evaluate its achievements, but it must always be based on scientific principles. The speaker has visited Europe and the United States twice and believes that they attach great importance to vocational guidance and that their methods are very suitable for their national conditions. However, Western and Chinese customs are different. To develop vocational guidance, we must use scientific methods and conduct thorough research. The promotion of vocational guidance requires investigation and statistics, so European and American vocational guidance agencies have a central statistics bureau. We must improve old professions and introduce new professions, and we must not engage in empty talk. We must combine society and education. Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, and Pan Yangyao's reports are omitted.

Constitution Adopted: (Article 1) The general assembly is organized by the Chinese Vocational Education Society in conjunction with vocational institutions nationwide to study matters relating to occupational guidance; (Article 2) All national organizations, universities, vocational schools, junior and secondary schools with occupational guidance organization or that pay attention to occupational guidance issues are eligible to join; (Article 3) The general assembly will hold an annual meeting, which is rotated and convened in different locations by the Executive Committee; (Article 4) Representatives of organizations are required to attend; (Article 5) The General Assembly elects 13 members to form an Executive Committee, which meets quarterly and is authorized to appoint experts to conduct research on occupational guidance issues; (Article 6) Application fee is divided into two types (Type A): pay ten yuan per year, (Type B) five yuan per year to be used for research, communication, printing, publishing and other activities by agencies which have joined; (Article 7) Agencies are allowed to ask questions or report their studies; (Article 8) Revisions of constitution can be made during the general assembly.

Resolution Adopted: One, all vocational guidance agencies should provide necessary contact and mutual assistance when they encounter difficulty in job placement and research to provide them with more convenient service; Two, vocational guidance agencies should jointly study methods of guidance to improve work efficiency; Three, vocational guidance agencies should recommend professional personnel to each other; Four, a request should be sent to each county's public education center to establish an occupational guidance department; Five, determine location, date and time for the General Assembly; Six, a decision should be made to hold the General Assembly in the capital; Seven, standard for occupational guidance should be defined; Eight, standard of procedures for occupational guidance in schools should be defined; Nine, standard table for vocational guidance should be defined; Ten, minimum level of organization for a vocational guidance organization should be defined. Eleven, amend the charter of the Chinese Vocational Guidance Organization. Twelve, Should the General Assembly consult with the Vocational Education Society to hold a regular meeting? Thirteen, How should the General Assembly publish its journal? Fourteen, Should the General Assembly organize an Executive Committee? The decision was made to organize an Executive Committee. Wu County Occupational Guidance Center, Wuxi Occupational Guidance Center, Nanjing Municipal Occupational Guidance Center, Jiading County Occupational Guidance Center, Datong University, Tongji University, Zhenjiang County Education Bureau, Hujiang University, Jiangsu Provincial Education College, National Central University, Vocational Introduction Department of the Youth Association, Vocational Introduction Department of the Chinese Engineering Society, and Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center were elected to form the Executive Committee with term until the General Assembly; Fifteen, All schools should set up free tuition for the impoverished students; Sixteen, How should folk schools guide the public with their occupations? Seventeen, Folk education facilities and farmer education facilities should place occupational guidance as a priority.

Friendly Football Match

French Army Wins Against Chinese B Mixed Team

Result: 4 to 3

The Shanghai Chinese Federation B mixed football team played a friendly match against the French Russo warship team at the Chinese baseball field yesterday. About two thousand people watched the game, making it the first grand occasion for the new autumn football season. As a result, the French army won with a score of 4 to 1.

First Half

The French team kicked off, and after about twenty minutes, the French right inside forward scored a goal against the Combined team. The Combined team then launched an aggressive attack, displaying remarkable prowess. The goalkeeper of the Combined team demonstrated agility, saving several dangerous shots, which was no easy feat. Later, the right inside forward of the Combined team shot, but the ball was blocked by the French goalkeeper. The center forward then knocked the goalkeeper to the ground, and the right inside forward scored, tying the score at 1-1. The French center forward, with strong kicking skills and both intelligence and courage, gained possession of the ball in midfield and dribbled past players, attacking directly at the defense. The Chinese team conceded another goal. At the end of the first half, the French team led 2-1.

Second Half

The French team's momentum waned slightly, and the Chinese team seized the opportunity to attack. The center forward scored, tying the score at 2-2. The Chinese team's morale soared, and they frequently lingered in the opponent's half. The right wing then scored another goal, giving them a 3-2 lead. However, before long, the French center forward performed another remarkable feat. At this time, the Chinese team repeatedly found themselves in dangerous situations and were eventually penalized with a twelve-yard kick. The French center forward gently flicked the ball, but it did not go into the goal. As the game was about to end, the French center forward, using his true skill, scored, making the final score 4-2 in favor of the French team.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Seafarer

Woman A: Oh dear! I broke a mirror. They say that means seven years of bad luck. What am I going to do? What am I going to do?

Woman B: Don't worry. Last year, my sister-in-law broke a mirror. She died less than half a year later. So she didn't even experience one year of the seven years of bad luck. What are you afraid of?

Pharmacist: In the middle of the night, disturbing my good dream. What serious illness has occurred?

Customer: I'm sorry. My wife is feeling unwell in her chest.

Pharmacist: Then she should drink a cup of plain boiled water. What medicine do you want to buy? Quick, tell me!

Customer: Thank you for reminding me. I'll go back and give her plain boiled water. I don't need to buy your medicine.

Man: My dear, this elopement of ours is no small matter. We must be careful about everything. We'll climb down from the window. Is that rope strong enough?

Woman: It doesn't matter. Anyway, my father and mother are holding it in the room for us. We certainly won't fall. If you're worried that the two of them aren't strong enough, we can ask my brother to help.

Ophthalmologist: Miss, you must apply this eye medicine three times a day. Don't forget.

Patient: Doctor, but there are rules for taking medicine. Some must be taken before meals, and some after meals. How should I apply this eye medicine?

Snapshots of the Japanese Depression

— Tsuru

Since the Hamaguchi Cabinet implemented the gold standard, the signs of economic depression in Japan have become increasingly apparent. In recent months, the number of unemployed in intellectual and labor circles has increased daily. Although authorities and political scholars have racked their brains to find countermeasures to the depression, they are merely stopgap measures and do not solve the problem.

The evil tide of the depression has swept across Japan. In newspapers, we see that people in many parts of Japan are eating tree bark and grass roots, just like the disaster victims in Shaanxi and Gansu in our country. Even in Tokyo, one of the world's five major metropolises, the economic depression is evident everywhere.

Nihonbashi, Kyobashi, and Ginza, a street about two Chinese miles long, is the most famous night market in Japan. The Japanese call it the "Street of Night." Every evening, when the lights come on, both sides of the street are filled with stalls selling all kinds of cheap goods. The crowds of tourists jostle shoulder to shoulder. Department stores on this street, such as Mitsukoshi and Matsuzakaya, all close at 9:00 PM. Looking down from these five-story buildings at the brightly lit, crowded streets, with trams and cars shuttling back and forth, one truly sees the beauty of the city. However, the night market on this street has now been eliminated by the times. When I went to visit the other day, I only saw scattered lights and stalls leaning haphazardly. Cars without passengers drove back and forth, calling out. Every ten minutes, I saw a lone tram slowly approaching from afar.

Next to the Kannon-do Hall in Asakusa District is a movie street. On this street, apart from two or three tobacco shops, the rest are all movie theaters or *shibai* (Japanese drama) theaters. I remember when I went there to see a play during the New Year last year, even though there was still an hour before the show started, all the theaters had "full house" signs hung up. But when I go back to look now, the scene has completely changed. About three-tenths of the hundred or so movie theaters have closed down. The remaining theaters that are still operating have added a promoter at the entrance. Whenever tourists pass by, they enthusiastically report on the day's program, how interesting the play is, and the big discounts, etc. However, the tourists seem to be made of iron and stone and are not moved by him at all.

There are fewer customers at various recreational places, but the number of visitors to libraries and parks has increased instead. The unemployed spend their days idly at home, so they go to public libraries to read magazines, pictorials, and newspaper advertisements. They stay there all day, not even coming out to eat. They are not forgetting to eat because they are engrossed in their studies, but because their pockets are empty. When they are tired at night, the park becomes their lodging.

Although national education is good, Japanese citizens, because they have no way to make a living, cannot help but take actions outside the law. Therefore, the number of theft and arson cases has recently broken Japan's new record. People starving and collapsing on the streets, unable to make a living, and killing their wives and committing suicide are heard of every day. The demon of depression is rampant. Let's see what methods they use to deal with it.

Antiquities Discovered in Shaanxi Province

— Ji Guan

According to a recent communication from a friend, Shaanxi Province is located in a remote mountainous area with obstructed transportation. Last month, a Northwest Scientific Expedition team happened to pass through the area and saw locals engaged in hunting. They discovered a yellow weasel's burrow. They dug vigorously downwards, reaching about five feet, when they suddenly felt something covering it horizontally. Upon inspection, it turned out to be ancient stone arrowheads, stone axes, stone knives, and other such items. They were covered in mottled moss and had an ancient appearance. There were a total of more than fifty pieces. The news spread like wildfire, and people rushed to see them. After being identified by the team members, they were determined to be relics from the late Neolithic Age and early Bronze Age before the Flood. They are about three thousand years old. At that time, China had not yet entered the era of written records.

In addition, more than two hundred bamboo slips of various sizes were discovered. Engraved at the top are era names such as Yuanshi, Yuankang, Dijie, and Shiyuan. The characters are all in Han clerical script, which is exceptionally elegant. They can serve as a reference material for historians. However, these objects were buried underground for nearly two thousand years. The reason they have lasted so long is due to the dry ground and the lack of rain throughout the year. It is said that the team has now completed its investigation and returned fully loaded. Their future contribution to science will certainly be significant.

Watching the Autumn Tide at Jiubao

— Zhang Qinghua

The autumn tide of the Qiantang River in Zhejiang is a famous spectacle in our province. Every year during the tidal season, countless tourists from home and abroad flock to see it. As a result, the remote Haining has become famous far and wide. However, the audience only knows Haining as the destination for watching the tide, and does not know that the area between Babao and Jiubao, about twenty miles east of Haining, is an even greater spectacle. The force of the tide is far greater than that at Haining, because the area happens to be where the southern tides meet. The two tides collide, constantly reaching heights of more than ten *zhang* (approximately 33 meters), swirling and descending into a curved shape, before regrouping and rushing towards Haining. Therefore, the occasional high tides that rise suddenly at Haining are actually the rebound of the aftershocks from the Babao area.

Last year, Zhu Jiahua, the Commissioner of Civil Affairs of Zhejiang Province, visited and appreciated the view with Yan Youfu, the Magistrate of Haining County. They marveled at the spectacle. This year, due to weather conditions, the tides are particularly fierce. More than a hundred *zhang* of the solid stone embankment in the area were destroyed by the tide. Even the new-style sloped stone embankment, built under the supervision of an Austrian engineer, was breached by the fierce tide. Moreover, near Jiubao East, the river tide actually crossed three tidal defense embankments and rushed into the inner river, Chenfen River. Even the Hangping Highway, about half a *li* (approximately 0.5 km) from the seawall, was broken by the incoming tide. Therefore, the force of the tide, the height of the collision, and the grandeur of the scene are all breathtaking. I record this to introduce it to the audience.

A Brief Biography of the Goddess

— Shen Hengzhuang

The most famous classical beauty on the American screen, Corinne Griffith, starred in a historical romantic sound drama for First National Company this spring. Its name is "The Divine Lady."

The plot of the drama is entirely based on the famous work "The Divine Lady" by the famous writer Barrington, and is adapted into a portrayal of the love affair between Nelson, the great English hero of the eighteenth century, and the beauty Emma Hamilton. It is extremely passionate and expresses the emotions to the fullest, becoming a historical costume sound drama that has never been seen before in the film industry.

In this film, Corinne plays the charming and gentle beauty Emma, looking even more beautiful than in her previous works. In short, First National Company's production of this film and Corinne's starring role in this drama can be called two great successes. It is said that the film is currently being screened at a summer peak.

Zeng Nongran's Cherishing of His Reputation

— Zheng Yimei

Zeng Nongran's passing has already been recorded by his peers. There are still some details that have not been fully explained, so I will elaborate further. Nongran, whose given name was Xi, was from Hengyang. His calligraphy was famous throughout the country. He would write sparsely on a fan or album, only a few lines, but with an antique and extraordinary air. Others, although they tried to imitate him, could not achieve the same effect. Sometimes he also engaged in painting. In the fans collected at the Xinhange Pavilion, I saw a landscape painting he made, which was vast and profound, directly approaching the ancients. It was rare to find his equal among contemporary artists. However, the painting was overshadowed by his reputation as a calligrapher, and few people knew about it. There was a person named Fang Langao, who was a fellow townsman of Nongran. Last year, Langao came to Shanghai for business and visited Nongran at his residence. Meeting a fellow townsman in a foreign land was an occasion for great joy. The weather was hot, and Langao waved a folding fan. Nongran took it to look at it and realized that it was his own handwriting, which he had given to Langao twenty years ago. He felt that his brushwork was immature and not worthy of being shown to others. Therefore, he asked Langao for it and tore it up. He spent the entire day creating a masterpiece to compensate him. Such was his meticulousness in cherishing his reputation. Nongran was also skilled in poetry, but he was dignified and did not deign to write about the love affairs of women. The Shanghai painter Zhang Shanzi created a "Twelve Beauties of Jinling" painting and asked him to write a poem for it. Nongran firmly refused. But when he read the painting, he realized that the so-called "Twelve Beauties of Jinling" were not about love affairs in boudoirs, but twelve tiger paintings of variegated colors. He repeatedly exclaimed "cunning" and wrote a poem for it with a smile. Nongran once stayed at an inn somewhere when a mutiny suddenly broke out. At night, soldiers went out to loot. The travelers were terrified and extinguished their candles, hiding in the dark corners. Nongran alone remained calm and unafraid, keeping his lamp brightly lit. He deliberately scattered his luggage and overturned his boxes, creating a chaotic scene as a diversion. The mutinous soldiers thought that there was nothing of value to plunder and did not even take a single thread. None of the other travelers were spared. They all praised his quick wit. Among the travelers, there was one who had run out of money and was in a predicament. Nongran instead helped him with funds so that he could return home quickly.

Travelogue of Nanyang (57)

— Linghua

On the 24th, I visited Yang Xiaotang, the new Consul of Penang, who is from Shanghai and speaks Cantonese. I was fortunate to meet him after he visited me yesterday. We talked about the situation when he first came to this place, emphasizing the importance of uniting Chinese and foreign friendship. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has now changed the regulations for overseas Chinese going abroad, requiring passports for both going abroad and returning home. Each passport costs eight yuan. The Consul has already issued a notice to the overseas Chinese. The regulations will take effect on June 1st. I don't know if there will be any obstacles to their implementation. Because ships depart every day, each ship carries thousands of Chinese people. If they must pay for a passport, it will also be a problem for the workers.

For people traveling to various states in British Malaya, passports are not usually required. Now, a passport is required to return to China, which the workers consider an additional burden. Those traveling to various ports in third-class cabins do not need a passport, but they must pay a head tax. It costs thirty yuan to go to Annam. Workers' luggage is confiscated upon arrival and must be redeemed with thirty yuan. It costs one hundred guilders to go to the Netherlands. Each guilder is equivalent to about one Shanghai silver dollar. This amount covers six months. If one does not leave the country within six months, it is confiscated. If one leaves the country, it is returned. It is said that it costs sixteen yuan per person to land in Luzon, and this amount will be increased. Moreover, they deliberately treat people harshly by inspecting their bodies and measuring their health, but this is just an excuse to create difficulties. People say that the Dutch used to treat the Japanese in this way, but when the Dutch went to Japan, the Japanese treated the Dutch in the same way. After that, the Dutch did not dare to treat the Japanese in this way, and they treated each other with courtesy. But they only treat the Chinese in this way. It is deplorable that a small country like the Netherlands mistreats the Chinese in this way. It is also said that Siam treats the Chinese entering the country very vexatiously. In the future, it will be difficult for the Chinese to go abroad. Alas!

On the 25th, I visited the Kek Lok Si Temple on Crane Mountain to see the various jade Buddha statues. When I first arrived in Nanyang, I felt a kind of interest, namely, jade Buddha statues. In Singapore, almost every temple has them. They are not made of jade, but of a white and lovely stone. The statues are also different from those in China and do not resemble Chinese people. Generally, Buddha statues differ according to the location. Japanese Buddha statues resemble Japanese people, Mongolian Buddha statues resemble Mongolians, and modern Indian Buddha statues resemble Indians. Therefore, the Buddha statues here are more realistic. Jade Buddha statues come in various sizes. Small ones cost one or two yuan, while large ones cost dozens or hundreds of yuan and are taller than people. Regardless of whether they are real or not, seeing their delicate eyebrows inspires a sense of transcendence. Kant's theory of aesthetics ultimately leads to disinterest. Buddha statues are deeply immersed in this samadhi, so they are the ultimate in beauty. Compared to today's bronze statues, which only express masculinity, they are more thought-provoking. I inquired about the origin of these statues. It is said that they are from Yangon, Myanmar. I have rarely seen jade Buddha statues in China for decades, except for the Jade Buddha Temple of Sheng Xuanhuai in Shanghai. This is because jade Buddha statues are rare in China. Efforts should be made to circulate these statues to various countries to transform the atmosphere of violence. I heard that the stone also varies in quality, and it would be even better if it were decorated with gold. It is different from the marble of Dali, Yunnan. If the Yunnan Road were open, it could also be made in Yunnan. I heard that this stone is also available in Ipoh, but there is not much of it.

Warmth in My Heart (282)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Sheds Tears, Her Heart Breaks; Crimson Lotus Fades, a Woman's Soul Departs

Zhang Yiqing turned around and thought that he was a little unfair to this woman. Although she is not uncomfortable now, in name, she is neither fish nor fowl. He had to try his best to comfort her for a while. The woman wiped her tears and said, "I have long had the intention for you to marry another person. After a person reaches middle age, they naturally always want to have a son under their knees. But unfortunately, I am not in good health and cannot bear children. If you marry someone else and she bears a son or daughter, that would be good. Your children will also be my children. I will certainly treat them the same way. You thought I would be jealous if you married someone else, so you hid it from me. You really don't know my heart; you have truly wronged me." Zhang Yiqing felt relieved after hearing this. He thought that she probably felt old and unattractive herself. Moreover, everyone is in middle age, and she has come to her senses. It is not just a robber having a change of heart; it is also the truth. He said, "I am very grateful that you can be so understanding. The reason I didn't tell you was not because I intended to hide it from you, but because you were sick. I was afraid that you would be unhappy and get sick from the anger. I thought it would be better to tell you slowly." The woman said, "But I have one idea; I don't know if you are willing to listen. My idea is that young people living outside are always a little uncared for. In the past, you hid it from me and didn't let your family know, so you had to rent a small house outside. Now that I already know, there is no need to hide it anymore. Why not bring her home? First, you don't have to run back and forth. Second, times are difficult now, and it will save a little money after all. Third, it will be more lively at home. Fourth, I am older than her after all and have eaten more years of rice. I can give her some pointers. She can also help me with household chores. People from their profession, to be honest, don't know anything about housekeeping at all. They can learn some rules of a proper family. Do you think I'm right?" Originally, when Zhang Yiqing heard her reveal his secret, his heart had been pounding. He thought there would be a big commotion. Because Zhang Yiqing had gone to brothels before and didn't come home, she had made a scene several times. Now, not only is she not making a scene, but she is also saying such pitiful things. He felt a little uneasy. Moreover, what she is saying at this moment is all upright and righteous. How could you ask for more? She allows you to marry a concubine, and when she comes, she is willing to guide and teach her. It couldn't be better. Running back and forth is not good. The expenses of two families are certainly greater. Her words are all very correct. Zhang Yiqing thought, now that everything is clear, of course, it is best to have Cuiyun move back.

The Origin of the Tight Money Market

Insufficient Silver Bullion Reserves Lead to Inadequate Minting of Silver Dollars for Supply

Since the surge in the price of gold in Shanghai, the abundance of silver on the market has been unprecedented. Fearing unusual market fluctuations, the government and municipal authorities prohibited the export of gold and the import of silver. This prevented foreign silver from entering Shanghai, leading to the shipment of large bars of Shanghai's silver reserves to Hong Kong and other ports. As a result, the money supply appeared superficially loose, but the actual silver reserves were far less than in previous years. Recently, due to anticipated rise in the exchange rate for silver dollars, financial circles requested the Hangzhou Mint to increase production. However, the lack of raw materials prevented full-scale minting. Consequently, only 240,000 silver dollars were minted daily. Although the output of silver dollars was limited, the daily demand for raw material in the form of large bars reached one hundred and several tens. This posed a significant logistical challenge, and the market supply fell far short of demand. As a result, the exchange rate for silver dollars remained high, and the shortage of raw material bars led to a tightening of the money supply. This, in turn, caused the rise in silver interest rates yesterday. However, industry insiders predict that the reopening of banks today (Monday) may ease the situation slightly.

Yesterday, American cotton was weak, first due to sales in the South, then slightly recovered due to purchases by industry peers. Futures fell one to six pounds per point, and spot prices fell five pounds per point. British cotton futures fell two to three points, now down seven points.
